[30;1m74 | [0m[35mclass Transformer(_Decoratable, ABC, Generic[_Leaf_T, _Return_T]):[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35m    """Transformers work bottom-up (or depth-first), starting with visiting the leaves and working[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35m    their way up until ending at the root of the tree.[0m
[30;1m77 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m78 | [0m[35m    For each node visited, the transformer will call the appropriate method (callbacks), according t[0m
[30;1m79 | [0m[35m    node's ``data``, and use the returned value to replace the node, thereby creating a new tree str[0m
